Keyboard-first parity (§V): the pure helper `buildUpdateActions(qualifies, latest, onUpdate, onDismiss): UpdatePaletteAction[]` (extracted to `lib/palette-update.ts` for unit-testability, mirroring `lib/palette-move.ts`) returns, when `qualifies && latest`:

- `{ id: "run-kit-update", label: `run-kit: Update to v${latest}`, onSelect: onUpdate }`
- `{ id: "run-kit-dismiss-update", label: "run-kit: Dismiss Update Notice", onSelect: onDismiss }`

and an empty array otherwise. **Gated on `qualifies` ALONE — the palette deliberately IGNORES chip dismissal** (`qualifies`, NOT the chip's `showChip`): dismissal silences the ambient chip, but the palette is deliberate discovery.

**Dual-mount duplication** (the board-palette convention, § Command Palette View actions → Dual-mount duplication): the app mounts TWO CommandPalettes and the board route does NOT render AppShell, so a globally-meaningful action must be registered in both.

- **AppShell palette** (`app.tsx`): an `updateActions` block (a `useMemo` over `buildUpdateActions`, alongside `viewActions`) folded into `paletteActions` after `configActions` and before `serverActions`. The update action wraps `updateNow` with a toast-on-failure handler (`"error"` severity).
- **Board palette** (`board-page.tsx` `boardRouteActions`): `buildUpdateActions` is duplicated in as `updateEntries`, appended near-last (since `260714-3law` the tail is `[...switchEntries, ...conditional, ...fontEntries, refreshEntry, helpEntry, ...updateEntries, ...maintenanceEntries]` — the maintenance entries follow the update entries, see below) — because below `sm` the top-bar UpdateChip is hidden, so on a phone `/board/$name` the palette is the ONLY update surface. (The board's toast call passes no severity arg, unlike AppShell's `"error"`.)

The Cockpit (`/`) mounts no palette, so it carries no update palette action (pre-existing scope-out — its chip still renders in the mode-invariant right cluster).

### Maintenance palette entries — `buildMaintenanceActions` (`lib/palette-update.ts`, `260714-3law-force-update-restart-palette`)

Two **palette-only** maintenance actions, independent of the qualifying-update gate that governs `buildUpdateActions` — they exist to make **patch-release update** and **daemon restart** reachable from the web (remote/mobile over Tailscale, no SSH), per Constitution V (keyboard-first) and IV (no new chrome). There is **no chip, no confirmation dialog, and no dedicated toast** — both fire immediately on select, and the SSE drop followed by the boot/version-driven tab reload IS the success feedback (only a rejection surfaces a toast).

The pure builder `buildMaintenanceActions(brew: boolean, version: string | null, onForceUpdate, onRestart): UpdatePaletteAction[]` (co-located with `buildUpdateActions` in `lib/palette-update.ts`, same test surface) computes `isDev = version === "dev"` and returns:

- `{ id: "run-kit-force-update", label: "run-kit: Update Now", onSelect: onForceUpdate }` — included ONLY when **`brew && !isDev`**. Force update (skips the qualify gate server-side), so it reaches patch releases and works before any check has run. Brew-gated because a non-brew install cannot self-upgrade (the backend brew 409 would reject it anyway).
- `{ id: "run-kit-restart", label: "run-kit: Restart Daemon", onSelect: onRestart }` — included whenever **`!isDev`** (**NO brew requirement** — restart works for any install method).

Neither appears on a `dev` daemon (both gated on `!isDev`). The existing qualifying-gated `run-kit: Update to v{latest}` entry (`buildUpdateActions`) is **unchanged** — a slight label overlap when an update qualifies is an accepted tradeoff (two static labels beat dynamic ones).

**Dual-mounted** per the same board-palette duplication convention as `buildUpdateActions` (below `sm` the top-bar chip cluster is hidden, so board routes on phones need palette parity — and there is no chip surface for these two at all):

- **AppShell** (`app.tsx`): a `maintenanceActions` `useMemo` over `buildMaintenanceActions(brew, daemonVersion, …)` (reading `brew`/`daemonVersion`/`forceUpdateNow`/`restartNow` from `useUpdateNotification()`), folded into `paletteActions` right after `updateActions`. Each action wraps `forceUpdateNow`/`restartNow` in a `.catch` toast-on-failure with **`"error"` severity** (messages `"Update failed"` / `"Restart failed"`).
- **Board** (`board-page.tsx` `boardRouteActions`): `maintenanceEntries` via the same builder + gating, appended **last** after `updateEntries`, with the same `.catch` toast handling but **no severity arg** (mirroring the board's existing `updateEntries` convention).

### Steady-state version surfaces (`260715-ifco-expose-running-version-ui`)

The `UpdateChip` above renders **only when a qualifying update is pending** and names only the TARGET version, so the running version is otherwise **invisible in the web UI** — a user filing a bug report or verifying a restart had to SSH in for `rk --version`. `260715-ifco` adds **four passive, chrome-level surfaces** that expose the *current* `daemonVersion` in steady state (frontend-only — the version already reaches every tab via `event: version`; no backend, no new routes/pages/buttons per Constitution IV, palette-first per V). All four **degrade gracefully on a null `daemonVersion`** (hide/omit, never a `vundefined` placeholder) and show the **`dev` sentinel as-is** (`run-kit dev`, not `vdev`) — pure display, unlike the dev-gated update/restart actions.

**Shared `displayVersion` helper + `lib/palette-version.ts`.** A new pure, dependency-free module `app/frontend/src/lib/palette-version.ts` (mirroring the `lib/palette-update.ts` pattern, colocated `palette-version.test.ts`) exports:

- **`displayVersion(version: string): string`** — the single frontend source of the v-prefix convention, mirroring the backend `displayVersion()` (`app/backend/cmd/rk/root.go:16-21`): prefixes `v` to a numeric version, leaves `dev` and any already-`v`-prefixed string bare (idempotent — never `vdev` / `vv0.6.2`). Reused by all three display surfaces below (avoids the magic-string conditional per-site). Chosen to live in the palette module rather than a standalone `lib/version.ts` — the palette builder already needs it and it is the new dependency-free home.
- **`buildVersionAction(version: string | null, onSelect: () => void): VersionPaletteAction[]`** — returns `[]` when `version` is null (omit, no placeholder), else a single `{ id: "run-kit-version", label: `run-kit: Version — ${displayVersion(version)}`, onSelect }`. The LABEL carries the version, so typing "version" in the palette answers "what am I on?" **without selecting anything**. `VersionPaletteAction` is a local type mirroring `palette-update.ts`'s shape.

**1. Command-palette version entry** (the primary discovery surface, §V). `buildVersionAction` is **dual-mounted** — the same board-palette duplication convention as the update actions (§ Dual-mount duplication), and for the same reason: below `sm` the top-bar right cluster is hidden, so on a phone `/board/$name` the palette is the ONLY version surface.
  - **AppShell** (`app.tsx`): a `versionActions` `useMemo` over `buildVersionAction(daemonVersion, …)`, folded into `paletteActions` **after `maintenanceActions`, before `serverActions`**.
  - **Board** (`board-page.tsx` `boardRouteActions`): `versionEntries` via the same builder, appended **last** after `maintenanceEntries` (`[...switchEntries, ...conditional, ...fontEntries, refreshEntry, helpEntry, ...updateEntries, ...maintenanceEntries, ...versionEntries]`).
  - **Gated on non-null `daemonVersion` INCLUDING `dev`** — `buildVersionAction`'s only gate is the null check (pure display; the entry is present for a `dev` daemon).
  - **On select**: copies the **DISPLAYED form** (`v0.6.2` / `dev` — what-you-see-is-what-you-copy, matches the label; NOT the raw `daemonVersion`) via `lib/clipboard.ts` `copyToClipboard`, then toasts. AppShell: `addToast(ok ? "Version copied" : "Copy failed", ok ? "info" : "error")`. Board: `addToast("Version copied", "info")` on success / `addToast("Copy failed")` (no severity arg) on failure — matching the board's own `updateEntries`/`maintenanceEntries` toast convention.

**2. Connection-dot version title** — the top-bar dot's hover `title` folds in `Connected — run-kit {displayVersion(daemonVersion)}`; full mechanics in § Chrome (Top Bar) → Connection dot.

**3. Cockpit footer stamp** (`server-list-page.tsx`) — a small passive BIOS/boot-style footer line `run-kit {displayVersion(daemonVersion)}` at the **bottom of the scroll container, after the SERVICES `</section>`** (out of the zone hierarchy — a POST-footer, on-brand with the CRT/terminal aesthetic). `text-xs text-text-secondary font-mono`, no border, no interaction, **no hover treatment** (passive means passive — the hover-animation vocabulary categories don't apply to inert text). Reads `daemonVersion` from `useSessionContext()` and renders **nothing when null** (`{daemonVersion && (…)}`, absence not a hidden placeholder). The Cockpit `/` is the only route with no top-bar version surface on phones, and its BIOS-footer aesthetic fits the stamp best.

**4. UpdateChip transition title** — the pending-update chip's `title`/`aria-label` now show `v{current} → v{latest}`; mechanics in § Top-bar L3 UpdateChip and the `current` field in § Context state + `useUpdateNotification()` hook.

**`copyToClipboard` success signal.** `lib/clipboard.ts` `copyToClipboard` was **widened from `Promise<void>` to `Promise<boolean>`** — `true` on a successful copy (Clipboard API OR the `execCommand` non-secure-context fallback), `false` when both fail (previously the total-failure branch silently swallowed the error). This is a **backwards-compatible** change: the pre-existing callers (`terminal-client.tsx`, `status-panel.tsx`) `void`-ignore the return and are unaffected; the new palette-version `onSelect` consumes the boolean to toast confirmation vs. error (honoring "fail soft with an error toast" in a non-secure context). The `copyToClipboard` return-value cases (Clipboard-API success, `execCommand`-fallback success, total failure) are unit-tested in `terminal-client.test.ts` (the pre-existing home of the `copyToClipboard` describe block — no separate `clipboard.test.ts` was added).

## Shell Grid Layout

The `<Shell>` wrapper (`app/frontend/src/components/shell/shell.tsx`) is the shared layout for `AppShell` and `BoardPage` (the Cockpit `/` uses a plain `flex-col h-full` instead — no Shell). **Since `260707-4vq2-lift-topbar-root-layout` the Shell grid NO LONGER carries a `topbar` row** — the TopBar is lifted out of every per-page grid and mounts once in the persistent root layout, full-width above the Shell (see § Chrome (Top Bar) → persistent root mount). Because the pre-`4vq2` grid already spanned the topbar full-width above the sidebar, dropping the row and painting the bar above Shell from the root layout is a **geometric no-op** — the visual stack (full-width bar over sidebar+content) is preserved.

The **desktop** (`≥ 640px`) grid is now just sidebar+content over bottombar:

```
gridTemplateAreas: "sidebar content" / "sidebar bottombar"   (rows: 1fr auto)
```

`gridTemplateColumns` stays `${sidebarWidth}px 1fr` when `sidebarOpen` else `0 1fr` (a `150ms ease-out` collapse transition, zero-width column when closed — no rail). The **mobile** (`< 640px`) branch is single-column `gridTemplateAreas: "content" "bottombar"` (rows `1fr auto`), with the sidebar rendered as an `absolute` overlay whose grid child spans `gridRow: "1 / 3"` (the content+bottombar rows, re-indexed from the pre-`4vq2` `"2 / 4"` now that the topbar row is gone — see § Sidebar Mobile). Children place themselves via `style={{ gridArea: … }}`.

**Shell height is `100%`** (was `var(--app-height, 100vh)` pre-`4vq2`) — Shell fills the root layout's `flex-1` content region rather than sizing itself to the viewport. Shell no longer calls `useVisualViewport()` or consumes `--app-height` directly (both moved to `RootWrapper` — see § iOS Keyboard Support). `useSidebarKeyboardToggle` (Cmd+\ / Ctrl+\) stays registered in Shell with unchanged behavior — the chord is live only on routes that mount a `<Shell>` (AppShell + BoardPage), as before.

**History**: since `260702-6m46-full-width-topbar-navbar` the topbar had spanned BOTH columns (`"topbar topbar" / "sidebar content" / "sidebar bottombar"`, rows `auto 1fr auto`, mobile `"topbar" "content" "bottombar"`); before `260702-6m46` it shared row 1 with the sidebar (`"sidebar topbar"`). `260707-4vq2` removed the row entirely and rewrote the `shell.tsx` ASCII topology comment to match.

## Chrome (Top Bar)

The full-width top bar is the app's primary chrome and doubles as the navbar. **Since `260707-4vq2-lift-topbar-root-layout` it mounts ONCE at the persistent root layout, above the router `<Outlet>` — not once per page** (see § Persistent root mount below). `TopBar` (`app/frontend/src/components/top-bar.tsx`) accepts a `mode: "terminal" | "board" | "root" | "cockpit"` prop (default `"terminal"`) selecting the left-nav content; the `260702-6m46-full-width-topbar-navbar` change added `"cockpit"` and turned the left nav into a breadcrumb bar. Everything below (per-mode breadcrumbs, center heading, right-cluster pyramid, connection dot) describes `TopBar`'s internal rendering, which `4vq2` did NOT touch — it relocated the mount only.

### Persistent root mount (`RootTopBar` / `AppLayout`, `260707-4vq2-lift-topbar-root-layout`)

Pre-`4vq2`, `TopBar` was mounted **three times** — once inside each page component (`AppShell` for `/$server` + `/$server/$window`, `ServerListPage` for `/`, `BoardPage` for `/board/$name`) — so cross-page navigation unmounted one instance and mounted a fresh one, a visible navbar "reload"/flicker (the app is already an SPA; this was a component-identity problem, not an MPA→SPA gap). `4vq2` lifts the bar to a single persistent mount that re-renders in place across route changes.

**Where it mounts.** A **pathless layout route** (`id: "app-layout"`, `router.tsx`) uniformly parents every page route (index, server, terminal, board), so every navigation keeps the match chain `[root, app-layout, <leaf>]`. Its component `AppLayout` (`app.tsx`) sits at a **stable match depth with a stable route id and is never remounted** across navigation; it renders a flex column — `<div className="app-root flex flex-col" style={{ height: "var(--app-height, 100vh)" }}>` — with `RootTopBar` in a `shrink-0` wrapper above a `flex-1 min-h-0` content region. The bar keeps a stable React identity and re-renders (props change, no unmount) as the URL flips. (Hosting the bar directly in `RootWrapper` — the root route's component — was tried and rejected: the index route `/` is a direct child of the root at the same pathname, making the root→index chain structurally shorter than root→serverLayout→…, so React remounted the root subtree on the index-route transition. The pathless layout normalizes tree depth and removes that asymmetry.) The `AppLayout` wrapper is a plain `div`, NOT `<header>` — `TopBar` already renders its own `<header>` banner landmark, so a second would nest two `role="banner"` landmarks.

**Suspense blast radius.** The `<Suspense fallback={null}>` boundary now wraps ONLY the `<Outlet>` content region (inside `AppLayout`), not the header. So when the lazy board chunk loads, only the page body blanks — the bar stays painted (fixing the second flicker cause without touching the lazy-loading strategy; `fallback={null}` itself is unchanged).

**Prop delivery — two channels.** `TopBar`'s inputs split by how synchronously they must resolve:

- **Route-derived (synchronous, at root)**: `RootTopBar` (`app.tsx`) derives `mode` + `boardName` from `useMatches()` — a deepest-first walk over route params (`window` ⇒ `terminal`, `name` ⇒ `board` + `boardName`, `server` ⇒ `root`, none ⇒ `cockpit`; param names are unique across the tree, the same walk `SessionContext` uses for `currentServer`). This flips the instant the URL changes, so the heading never waits on the incoming page's mount — critical for the lazy board (`Board: <name>` renders from the URL param while the chunk still loads). `mode`/`boardName` are deliberately NOT in the slot.
- **Page-registered (a slot context, `contexts/top-bar-slot-context.tsx`)**: pages publish their data/handler props — `sessions`, `currentSession`, `currentWindow`, `sessionName`, `windowName`, `isConnected`, `sidebarOpen`, `server`, `onNavigate`, `onToggleSidebar`, `onCreateSession`, `onCreateWindow`, plus board extras (`paneCount`, `serverCount`, `waitingPaneCount`, `boards`, `onCloseFocused`, `closeDisabled`, and — `260708-738w` — `autofit`/`onToggleAutofit` for the board autofit toggle, § Board Autofit Toggle) — via `useRegisterTopBarSlot(...)` (an effect: publish on mount/update, **clear to `null` on unmount**, last-writer-wins). This follows the `FocusedTerminalProvider` precedent (referentially-stable dispatcher held in a `useRef`, `useMemo`'d context value) and keeps the heavy handlers where they live — `AppShell`'s `navigateToWindow` (View-Transitions gate) and `handleCreateSessionInstant` (optimistic ghosts) are published by reference; **no logic migrates to root**.

**Tolerant-empty defaults.** When no page has registered yet (first frame after navigation, or a lazy chunk still loading), the slot value is `null` and `RootTopBar` renders the route-derived mode with the tolerant-empty prop shape every `TopBar` mode already supports (`sessions=[]`, `currentSession=null`, `currentWindow=null`, `sessionName/windowName/server=""`, `sidebarOpen=false`, no-op callbacks). No crash, no stale props from the prior page (the clear-on-unmount guarantees this).

**Not-found is a dedicated boolean channel.** `TopBarSlotContext` carries a `notFound` flag SEPARATE from the page-data `slot`. `NotFoundPage` (`router.tsx`) — the `app-layout` route's `notFoundComponent`, rendered inside the `<Outlet>` below the persistent bar — calls `useSignalTopBarNotFound()` (sets `true` on mount / `false` on unmount); `RootTopBar` reads `useTopBarNotFound()` and forces `mode="cockpit"` (nulling `boardName`) BEFORE the route-param walk. This is required because TanStack Router's fuzzy not-found handling RETAINS the partially-matched params in `useMatches()` (e.g. `/board/x/y` keeps `name=x`), so the param walk alone would derive `board` mode ("Board: x") over the not-found body. A separate boolean (vs. folding into the page-data slot, or reading the router's internal `globalNotFound`) keeps `NotFoundPage` — which owns no TopBar data — from publishing the full slot shape, and avoids coupling to a router-internal field + hardcoded route-id string. Because `RootTopBar` sits ABOVE the `<Outlet>`, the in-Outlet signal is inherently one render behind: a ~1-frame "Board: x" flash before the effect lands is unavoidable without reading router internals — not user-perceptible, and the settled state (A-015) is unaffected. (The `/a/b/c` shape is a DIFFERENT arm: it renders `AppShell`'s `ServerNotFound` early-return, not `NotFoundPage`, so `notFound` stays false there and the `root`/`terminal` mode derivation is kept.)

**Per-page removal.** Each page dropped its `<TopBar>` mount and registers instead: `AppShell` deleted its `<header style={{ gridArea: "topbar" }}><TopBar/></header>` block and its `topBarMode` local (the `terminal` vs `root` distinction is now derived at root); `ServerListPage` deleted its `<TopBar mode="cockpit"/>` mount + import and registers just `isConnected: hostMetricsConnected` (its wrapper `flex flex-col h-screen` → `h-full`); `BoardPage` deleted its board `<header>…<TopBar mode="board"/>` block (kept the `HELP_URL` import for its palette action) and registers the board extras (`boardName`, counts, `boards`, `onCloseFocused: unpinFocused`, `closeDisabled`, `isConnected: boardConnected`). Edge pages (`NotFoundPage`, `ServerNotFound`, `ServerWaiting`) changed their centering wrapper `h-screen` → `h-full` so they fit the content region below the persistent bar without overflow.

**Achievable-invariant note (e2e).** No component in the persistent chain (`RootWrapper`/`AppLayout`/`RootTopBar`/`TopBar`) remounts across navigation, so the flicker is gone and the bar stays continuously present with a per-route heading — this is what `tests/e2e/top-bar-persistence.spec.ts` asserts (mount-effect stability + per-route heading), NOT strict DOM-node identity. TanStack Router 1.168's per-match Suspense re-commit recreates the header host node on the `→ /` (index-route) transition; that is a router-internal reconciliation artifact that does NOT remount the component and does NOT blank the bar (the heading renders synchronously from route state), so it is not a user-visible flicker. The spec's brand-crumb hop is a RELOAD BOUNDARY — the brand is a raw `<a href="/">` TanStack Router does not intercept, a full document navigation — so only the client-side hops carry the no-remount claim.

**Non-goals.** Sidebar/BottomBar/Shell stay per-page (they still remount on `/$server` ↔ `/board/$name`); `TopBar`'s internal rendering across all four modes is unchanged; frontend-only (no backend/API/tmux change).

`app.tsx` and `board-page.tsx` no longer render `<TopBar>` directly; `server-list-page.tsx` (Cockpit `/`) no longer pins it above its own scroll container. All three now register into the slot context (see § Persistent root mount above). The right-section control cluster is a **strict 3-level cumulative pyramid** (`260704-9o7k-top-bar-button-pyramid`): a stable always-block pinned right renders in every mode, with terminal+board extras and terminal-only extras growing leftward — so no shared button ever changes screen position between pages. Only which levels appear gates on mode; see § Right cluster below.

**Layout** (`border-b-[3px] border-border` — a 3px structural seam, see § Border-Width System): a single line, a **3-column CSS grid `grid grid-cols-[1fr_auto_1fr] items-center gap-2 py-2`** (since `260703-5ilm-window-heading-hover-vocabulary` replaced the former `flex justify-between`). The grid is the load-bearing change: `1fr auto 1fr` makes the CENTER cell truly centered regardless of asymmetric left/right widths, which `flex justify-between` could not do. LEFT cell = `<nav aria-label="Breadcrumb">` (ends at the parent — see per-mode below); CENTER cell = the **universal `PageType: name` page heading, FILLED IN EVERY MODE** since `260704-pr0p-navbar-page-heading-boot-sweep` (terminal `WindowHeading` + ▾ window switcher / board display heading + ▾ board switcher / root display heading / solo `Cockpit` — the cell is no longer empty on root/board/cockpit; § Chrome (Top Bar) center cell); RIGHT cell = the control cluster (`justify-self-end`). No Line 2. The header itself carries `px-3` (the center cell is `flex items-center justify-center min-w-0`, no flex `gap` — the boot sweep owns the prefix→name spacing via its own space cell).

**Brand root crumb** (all modes, left-most): the logo icon (`/icon.svg`, always visible) + `hidden sm:inline` "Run Kit" wordmark wrapped in a single `<a href="/">` (`aria-label="Run Kit home"`). This IS the home affordance — there is no separate "Cockpit" crumb, and the old right-side "Run Kit" anchor is GONE (moved here by `260702-6m46`). The brand carries the `LINK_CRUMB_CLASS` bordered-chip treatment (see § Crumb Affordance Vocabulary). Below `sm` it collapses to the bare icon so long crumbs still fit the single-line 375px topbar.

**Hamburger** — the sidebar toggle (`aria-label="Toggle navigation"`, a Notion-style rounded-rect pictogram whose left column fills when `sidebarOpen`). Renders BETWEEN the brand and the first crumb, on every mode that has a sidebar. `hasSidebar` is DERIVED as `mode !== "cockpit"` (no separate prop) — cockpit is the only sidebar-less mode, so it gets no hamburger.

**Separator** — `›` (U+203A, `aria-hidden`, `BreadcrumbSeparator`), the established palette-label convention (`<session> › <name>`). It replaced the old `/` plain-text separator (removed by `260702-6m46`) between every crumb level. No `/` separator remains.

**Cockpit** (`/`, `mode="cockpit"`): brand crumb ONLY — no hamburger, no crumbs, no terminal-font control, no split/close buttons, and **no fixed-width button** (terminal-only since `260704-9o7k`; the 900px effect never applied to the Cockpit — `server-list-page.tsx` never reads `fixedWidth`). Renders only the L3 always-block (Notification / Theme / Refresh / Help) **plus the connection dot**, which since `260704-9o7k` reflects **host-metrics stream health** (formerly hidden here on the premise "no per-server SSE stream"; the Cockpit's live data actually arrives via the dedicated `?metrics=1` stream or the per-server metrics fan-out — `server-list-page.tsx` passes `hostMetricsConnected` from `useSessionContext()`, replacing the old `isConnected={false}`; see § Right cluster → connection dot and architecture.md § Server-independent host-metrics subscription). Session/server-dependent props are passed empty (`sessions=[]`, `currentSession=null`, `currentWindow=null`, `sessionName=""`, `server=""`, no-op callbacks) — the same tolerant-empty shape board mode uses. The Cockpit's page identity is the **solo `Cockpit` heading in the top-bar center cell** since `260704-pr0p` (a `PageHeadingDisplay` with `prefix=""` + `name="Cockpit"` + `solo` — primary-medium, visible at all breakpoints; § center cell). The former in-page `[ cockpit ]` `PageHeading` row is GONE. "Run Kit cockpit" was rejected — it would duplicate the adjacent brand crumb.

**Server Cabin** (`/$server`, no `$window`, `mode="root"`): the left breadcrumb ends at **brand + hamburger** — nothing more. Since `260704-pr0p-navbar-page-heading-boot-sweep` the server name is the **`Server Cabin: <server>` heading in the CENTER cell** (a display-only `PageHeadingDisplay`, no rename), NOT a left-nav leaf. The former `260702-6m46` root leaf — a non-link `<span aria-current="page">` server name (which had itself replaced the deleted literal "Dashboard" label) — was REMOVED from the left nav (move-don't-copy: the current-page leaf is the centered heading; a name never appears twice in the bar). "Dashboard" still appears nowhere.

**Terminal** (`/$server/$window`, `mode="terminal"`): the breadcrumb is brand + hamburger + `›` + server link + `›` + **session dropdown — and ENDS THERE** (since `260703-5ilm` the window identity moved OUT of the breadcrumb chain into the centered `WindowHeading`; the former trailing `›` + window dropdown are gone from the left nav). The server crumb here is a plain `<a href="/$server">` (a link back to the Server Cabin, `LINK_CRUMB_CLASS` chip, `truncate max-w-[16ch]`) — NOT a dropdown (server switching stays in the command palette, `Server: Switch to …`). The session crumb keeps its existing `BreadcrumbDropdown` behavior unchanged (session switch jumps to the session's first window; `+ New Session` action; session `max-w-[16ch] truncate` (matches the server crumb); the session name is snapshot-derived from the active `@N`, not a URL segment, since `260529-jad6`). **The window switcher relocated to the center cell** — a label-less bare-`▾` `BreadcrumbDropdown` (still `title="Window"`, still `windowItems` + `+ New Window` action) sitting beside the `WindowHeading` (name-click = edit, `▾`-click = switch), so the window name is never duplicated in one bar. Since `260704-pr0p` the centered `WindowHeading` gains a static prefix sibling span (§ Window Heading) — the two-tone `PageType: name` identity, `Window:` in every lens since `260714-uco1` — but the breadcrumb shape is otherwise unchanged (this is the only mode whose left nav did NOT lose a leaf to the generalized move-don't-copy rule, because it already ended at the session crumb). See § Chrome (Top Bar) center cell / § Breadcrumb Dropdowns → Window switcher. No type-prefix words ("SERVER"/"Cabin"/"session") — crumbs are instance names only; position conveys the level. The level IS named on hover via native `title` tooltips in the canonical vocabulary: brand `title="Cockpit"`, server crumb `title="Server Cabin"` (both link and leaf variants), session dropdown trigger `title="Session"` and the relocated window switcher `title="Window"` (via BreadcrumbDropdown's optional `title` prop).

**Center cell — the universal `PageType: name` page heading** (`260703-5ilm` introduced it terminal-only; `260704-pr0p-navbar-page-heading-boot-sweep` FILLED IT ON EVERY MODE). The outer center `<div className="flex items-center justify-center min-w-0">` (no flex `gap` — the boot sweep's own `sp` space cell separates prefix from name; a `gap-1` on top double-spaced them, `260704-pr0p` rework N4) stays centered in the grid; since `260714-uco1` it wraps an **inner anchor `<div className="flex items-center justify-start min-w-0 sm:min-w-[28ch]">`** — a `sm:`-gated min-width with LEFT-aligned content so the heading's left edge stops drifting as the instance name length changes (below `sm` the min-width is absent — space is scarce at 375px). The browser-history arrows + hierarchy ▾ live INSIDE this anchored box (§ Center-heading stable anchor + nav affordances). It renders per mode:

- **terminal** (`mode === "terminal" && currentWindow`): `<HistoryNav>` ◀ ▶ + `<HierarchyDropdown mode="terminal">` (left of the prefix) + `<WindowHeading>` (static `Window: <window>`, editable name — see § Window Heading) + the relocated bare-`▾` window switcher.
- **board** (`mode === "board" && boardName`): `<HistoryNav>` + `<HierarchyDropdown mode="board">` + a `<PageHeadingDisplay prefix="Board:" name={boardName}>` (display-only — boards have no rename API) + the `<BoardSwitcher>` ▾ (moved here from the left `BoardModeBreadcrumb`).
- **root** (`mode === "root" && server`): `<HistoryNav>` + `<HierarchyDropdown mode="root">` + `<PageHeadingDisplay prefix="Server Cabin:" name={server}>` (display-only).
- **cockpit**: `<HistoryNav>` + `<PageHeadingDisplay prefix="" name="Cockpit" solo>` — a solo type word, no instance name, primary-medium, visible at all breakpoints; NO hierarchy ▾ (the root has no ancestors).

The type-prefix constants live once in `top-bar.tsx`: `WINDOW_PREFIX = "Window:"` (`260714-uco1`, replacing the retired `TERMINAL_PREFIX`/`terminalHeadingPrefix()`/`WEB_PREFIX`/`CHAT_PREFIX`), `BOARD_PREFIX = "Board:"`, `CABIN_PREFIX = "Server Cabin:"`, `COCKPIT_SOLO = "Cockpit"` (title case, superseding PageHeading's lowercase idiom). Because the cell lives in the `auto` middle grid column, it stays centered under the topbar regardless of the breadcrumb / control-cluster widths. The `WindowHeading` (and the display headings) are deliberately NOT keyed on the route identity (no remount `key`) so they persist across window/page switches — that is what lets the boot sweep replay on navigation and keeps an in-progress inline edit alive (an external windowId/server switch mid-edit CANCELS the stale edit instead, since committing the typed name onto the newly-navigated window would rename the wrong one — the equivalent of the retired modal being pinned to the window it opened on).

### Center-heading stable anchor + nav affordances (`260714-uco1`)

Four affordances added to the top-bar center heading by `260714-uco1-topbar-heading-anchor-nav`, all inside the anchored center box (§ Chrome (Top Bar) center cell), no new routes and no backend surface:

- **Stable left anchor.** The outer center cell stays `justify-center` in the grid; an INNER container `flex items-center justify-start min-w-0 sm:min-w-[28ch]` reserves a `sm:`-gated min-width with LEFT-aligned content, so the heading's left edge stops drifting as the instance name length changes (min-width chosen over fixed-width+truncate — long names grow rightward, accepted). Applies uniformly across all four modes; below `sm` the min-width is absent (unchanged 375px behavior). The `28ch` value is monospace-exact (`Window: ` is 2ch shorter than the old `Terminal: `), visually tuned. The inline-rename `<input>` is `text-left` (was `text-center`) so the name does not jump on edit entry (§ Window Heading → edit).
- **Hierarchy ▾ dropdown** (`HierarchyDropdown`, reuses `BreadcrumbDropdown`). A bare-`▾` sibling of the rename button, bound LEFT of the prefix (reads `▾ Window: name`), listing EXACTLY the current page's ANCESTOR chain — no lateral jumps. Terminal: `Server Cabin: {server}` (→ `/{server}`) then `Cockpit` (→ `/`); board & root: `Cockpit` only; **solo Cockpit: not rendered** (the root has no ancestors). `hidden sm:inline-flex` — below `sm` it rides with the hidden prefix span (the hamburger/sidebar covers mobile nav). Being a sibling of the rename button, clicking it never enters inline edit. Navigation routes through the typed `useNavigate()` (params validated). Known/accepted redundancy with the left breadcrumb (deferred — out of scope).
- **Browser-history ◀ ▶ arrows** (`HistoryNav`). Fixed-width bordered `rk-glint` icon buttons (`coarse:` touch sizing, `aria-label`s) rendered LEFT of the prefix inside the anchored box on ALL FOUR modes (history is global). They call TanStack Router's `useRouter().history.back()` / `.forward()` — BROWSER HISTORY, explicitly NOT sibling-window cycling. Being fixed-width they never shift the heading's text anchor. Forward is always-active (browser-chrome style — `canGoForward` is not reliably exposed, so a dim/disabled state is best-effort and omitted; a no-forward click is a harmless no-op).
- **`Go:` palette parity** (Constitution V) via the pure `lib/palette-nav.ts` builder `buildNavActions(mode, server, handlers)` (+ colocated `palette-nav.test.ts`), mirroring `palette-move.ts`/`palette-view.ts`. Returns the two history actions (`Go: Back`/`Go: Forward`, ALWAYS) followed by the route-appropriate ancestor entries (`Go: Server Cabin` when `mode === "terminal" && server`; `Go: Cockpit` for terminal/board/root). `app.tsx`'s `navActions` `useMemo` wires it into the `paletteActions` composition, passing `router.history.back/forward` + `navigate(...)` bodies, with `mode = windowParam ? "terminal" : "root"` — AppShell never passes `"board"`/`"cockpit"`, so the builder's `NavMode` `"board"`/`"cockpit"` values have no production call site (plan-recorded deletion candidate: either wire `buildNavActions("board", …)` into `boardRouteActions` or narrow the type). No new app-level keybindings (browser-native Alt+←/→ already cover history).

**Board** (`/board/$name`, `mode="board"`): the left breadcrumb is brand + hamburger + a **counts/hint span ONLY** (`BoardModeInfo` — `{N} pane[s] · {M} server[s] · ⌘[⌘] cycle`, no leading `›` because the hint is not a crumb). Since `260704-pr0p-navbar-page-heading-boot-sweep` the board name + ▾ switcher MOVED to the center heading (`Board: <board>` display + `<BoardSwitcher>`; § center cell), and the former left `Board ▸` home button is GONE (the brand crumb is already the home affordance, and a left `Board` word would duplicate the centered type word — move-don't-copy). This reduced the old `260702-6m46` `BoardModeBreadcrumb` (`Board ▸ {name} ▾ {counts}`) to just its counts/hint tail. Right cluster: the L2 controls (Aa + the board-only **autofit toggle** between Aa and ✕ + ✕, where the ✕ **unpins the focused pane** — see § Right cluster / § Close pane button / § Board Autofit Toggle) and the L3 always-block including the connection dot, which since `260704-9o7k` shows an **AND over the board's attached servers** (green iff ≥1 entry AND every distinct attached server's `isConnectedByServer` slice is connected; `board-page.tsx` derives `boardConnected` and passes it, replacing the old `isConnected={false}`). (Board mode no longer hides the dot — the `260704-9o7k` change dropped that gate.)

**Mobile (`< sm`)** — the brand collapses to the bare icon and intermediate crumbs (server link + session, plus their `›` separators, wrapped in `hidden sm:flex` spans) are hidden, leaving brand icon + the centered heading. Since `260704-pr0p` the leaf is the **center-cell heading in EVERY mode** (no longer just Terminal): Terminal → `WindowHeading` (the mobile leaf AND primary rename affordance, `coarse:min-h-[30px]` touch target), Server Cabin → the `Server Cabin: <server>` display heading, Board → the `Board: <board>` display heading, Cockpit → the solo `Cockpit`. **The two-tone `PageType:` prefix is hidden below `sm`** (`hidden sm:inline`) so mobile keeps just the name — EXCEPT the solo `Cockpit` word (a name-equivalent, not a prefix), which stays visible at all breakpoints. The `▾` window/board switcher stays visible on mobile with its `+ New Window` / board-switch action. Long names truncate in the center cell (`max-w-[16ch]` on mobile, `sm:max-w-[28ch]`) — never wrap or squeeze neighbors. The topbar stays a single line at 375px (the documented invariant in `fab/project/context.md`).

**Right cluster** (`flex items-center gap-3`, `justify-self-end`) — a **strict 3-level cumulative pyramid** (`260704-9o7k-top-bar-button-pyramid`), growing LEFTWARD from a stable always-block pinned right, so no shared button ever changes screen position between pages:

| Level | Gate | Buttons (left → right) |
|---|---|---|
| **L1** — terminal only | `currentWindow` set (`mode === "terminal"`) | SplitButton (vertical) · SplitButton (horizontal) · **FixedWidthToggle** |
| **L2** — terminal + board | `mode === "terminal" \|\| mode === "board"` | TerminalFontControl (Aa) · **BoardAutofitToggle (board-only, between Aa and ✕)** · **ClosePaneButton (✕)** |
| **L3** — always (all four modes) | none | **UpdateChip (⬆ v… — leading, conditional: hidden unless a qualifying, un-dismissed, non-dev update is pending — `260713-4zap`)** · NotificationControl (🔔) · ThemeToggle (◐) · **RefreshButton (⟳)** · HelpLink (?) · **connection dot (●)** |

Each control sits in a `hidden sm:flex` span (the whole cluster is desktop-only — mobile hides it) and carries the shared `rk-glint` chip styling (`min-w-[24px] min-h-[24px] coarse:min-w-[30px] coarse:min-h-[30px]`). L1's absence on non-terminal pages just widens the gap to the breadcrumb; the L3 always-block keeps its fixed right edge (the brand anchor moved to the left nav as the root crumb — `260702-6m46`). Deltas `260704-9o7k` introduced from the prior "mostly mode-invariant" cluster:

- **L3 order is user-specified**: Notification → Theme → Refresh → Help, then the dot as the **right-most status terminator** (not a button). Since `260713-4zap` the conditional **UpdateChip leads the block** (Update → Notification → Theme → Refresh → Help → dot) — it renders only when a qualifying, un-dismissed, non-`dev` update is pending, so its absence just tightens the gap (§ Update Notification).
- **RefreshButton promoted** L1 → L3 (was terminal-only; now renders in every mode — a reload is meaningful everywhere; behavior unchanged: plain click `window.location.reload()`, Shift+click `forceReload()`). See § Refresh button.
- **FixedWidthToggle demoted** always → L1 (now terminal-only). Its *behavior* is untouched: the 900px `maxWidth` wrapper lives in AppShell (`app.tsx`), which renders both `terminal` AND `root`, so **Server Cabin keeps the constraint and the `View: Fixed Width` palette access** — only the Cabin button is removed (it was already a no-op on Board/Cockpit, which never read `fixedWidth`). See § Command Palette View actions.
- **TerminalFontControl (Aa)** gating simplified from `mode !== "root" && mode !== "cockpit"` to the L2 predicate `mode === "terminal" || mode === "board"` (same effective result — a terminal-bearing surface: the single window or a board pane).
- **ClosePaneButton (✕) is now mode-aware** (one component, DD-1): terminal ✕ kills the active pane (`closePane`); board ✕ **unpins the focused pane** (non-destructive). See § Close pane button.
- **BoardAutofitToggle is board-only, INSIDE L2** (`260708-738w`): a new toggle rendered **between Aa and ✕** in the L2 cluster, but gated `mode === "board" && onToggleAutofit` (narrower than the L2 predicate — it does NOT appear on terminal). Mirrors `FixedWidthToggle` (`aria-pressed`, `rk-glint`, `coarse:` sizing) and flips the per-board desktop autofit preference. See § Board Autofit Toggle.

**Connection dot** (`role="status"`, `aria-live="polite"`, green `bg-accent-green` / gray `bg-text-secondary`, `aria-label` Connected/Disconnected) — the right-most element, now in **ALL four modes** (`260704-9o7k` dropped the former `mode !== "board" && mode !== "cockpit"` gate). Since `260715-ifco-expose-running-version-ui` it also carries a hover **`title`** that folds in the running version — a computed `dotTitle`: `Disconnected` when `!isConnected`, else `Connected — run-kit {displayVersion(daemonVersion)}` when `daemonVersion` is known, else bare `Connected` (the version fragment is OMITTED until the first `event: version` so the title is never `vundefined`). `daemonVersion` is read via `useUpdateNotification()` (already imported for the UpdateChip); `displayVersion` from `lib/palette-version`. The **`aria-label` stays the concise `Connected`/`Disconnected`** — the version is hover-discovery detail, not screen-reader-essential state on the live region. Its meaning is per-page "this page's live data is flowing", derived by each caller and passed as `isConnected`:

- **Terminal / Server Cabin**: unchanged — the current server's SSE stream (`isConnectedByServer.get(server)` mirrored through ChromeProvider).
- **Cockpit**: host-metrics stream health — `hostMetricsConnected` from `useSessionContext()` (dedicated `?metrics=1` stream health when no server is attached, else derived from per-server metrics fan-out; architecture.md § Server-independent host-metrics subscription).
- **Board**: `boardConnected` — AND over the board's attached servers (green iff ≥1 entry AND every distinct attached server's slice is connected).

**Help link** (`HelpLink` in `top-bar.tsx`; `260704-hmd0-help-icon-top-bar`): an external-docs chip in the L3 always-block, after `RefreshButton` (since `260704-9o7k` inserted Refresh between Theme and Help) and before the connection dot (in the same `hidden sm:flex` span as the sibling controls). An **`<a>`, not a button** — it navigates externally to the exported `HELP_URL` constant (`https://shll.ai/run-kit`) with `target="_blank"` + `rel="noopener noreferrer"`, so the live dashboard (terminals, SSE) is never unloaded. Carries the shared cluster chip styling verbatim (`rk-glint` glint hover + `min-w-[24px] min-h-[24px] coarse:min-w-[30px] coarse:min-h-[30px] rounded border border-border text-text-secondary hover:border-text-secondary`) and a 14px inline `currentColor` `?` SVG glyph matching the sibling icons; `aria-label`/`title` "Help — run-kit docs". `HELP_URL` is defined once in `top-bar.tsx` (mirroring the `NOTIFICATIONS_HELP_URL` precedent) and **exported** so the palette action reuses the same constant — the two cannot drift. The palette counterpart is the `Help: Documentation` action (`id: "help-documentation"`), registered in `app.tsx`'s `configActions` next to `Help: Keyboard Shortcuts` — so it reaches the **AppShell palette only** (Terminal + Server Cabin), NOT the board route's own `boardRouteActions` (which carries only `refresh-page` + the terminal-font trio) and NOT the Cockpit (mounts no palette). **The chip itself renders on every route** (mode-invariant right cluster); it is only the *palette* affordance that is AppShell-scoped. Unit-tested in `top-bar.test.tsx` (asserts `href`, `target="_blank"`, `rel` containing `noopener`, and an accessible name); no dedicated e2e — a static anchor in existing chrome has no interactive flow to drive.

**Split buttons** (`SplitButton` in `top-bar.tsx`): Two inline components calling `splitWindow(server, windowId, horizontal, cwd)` from `api/client.ts`. The active `server` is passed as a prop from `TopBar` (read from `useSessionContext()` at handler scope). Custom SVG icons (square-split pattern). Best-effort error handling — tmux may reject if pane is too small. `POST /api/windows/{windowId}/split` with `{ "horizontal": bool }`.

**Close pane button** (`ClosePaneButton` in `top-bar.tsx`): the L2 ✕ chip — **mode-aware via optional props, one component** (`260704-9o7k`, DD-1: reuses the single chip styling/spinner rather than a second `UnpinFocusedButton`). Props: `server?`, `windowId?`, `onUnpin?: () => void`, `disabled?: boolean`, `label = "Close pane"`. Two behaviors:
- **Terminal** (default, no `onUnpin`): the optimistic kill path — `closePane(server, windowId)` via `useOptimisticAction`, spinner (`LogoSpinner`) + `disabled` while pending. Kills the active pane of the current window; targets via `POST /api/windows/{windowId}/close-pane`. Rendered only when `currentWindow` exists. Also available as "Pane: Close" in the command palette.
- **Board** (`onUnpin` provided, `260704-9o7k`): calls `onUnpin` — synchronous **unpin of the board's focused pane** (a non-destructive move-out, NOT a tmux kill; kill stays in each pane's own UI, because a top-bar button that killed whatever agent happens to be focused is an expensive misclick). No spinner (`busy` is forced `false` when `onUnpin` is set). Board wiring (`board-page.tsx`) passes the board-specific `label="Unpin pane from board"` (used for both `aria-label` and `title`, distinct from the terminal "Close pane") and `disabled` (`closeDisabled = entries.length === 0`, so the ✕ is disabled on a zero-pane board).

X-shaped close icon SVG (`width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 24 24"`), shared `rk-glint` chip styling. Hidden on mobile (`hidden sm:flex`). The board `onUnpin` is wired from `board-page.tsx` as `unpinFocused` (`unpin(entries[focusedIndex].server, .windowId, name)`, reusing the existing `POST /api/boards/{name}/unpin` — no backend change), and mirrored to the palette as `Board: Unpin Focused Pane` for keyboard parity (§ Boards Command Palette).

**Board autofit toggle** (`BoardAutofitToggle` in `top-bar.tsx`; `260708-738w-board-autofit`): the L2 cluster's **board-only** toggle, rendered **between `Aa` (`TerminalFontControl`) and `✕` (`ClosePaneButton`)** but gated on `mode === "board" && onToggleAutofit` (narrower than the terminal+board L2 predicate — it never renders on the Terminal route). Props: `autofit: boolean`, `onToggle: () => void`. Mirrors the `FixedWidthToggle` vocabulary — `aria-label="Toggle board autofit"`, `aria-pressed={autofit}`, shared `rk-glint` glint hover + `coarse:` touch sizing, `title` reflecting on/off ("Autofit on (panes fill the row)" / "Autofit off (fixed pane widths)"). Clicking it flips the per-board desktop autofit preference; the palette counterpart `Board: Toggle Autofit (on/off)` flips the SAME state (Constitution V parity). It is wired from `BoardPage` through the top-bar slot context (`autofit` + `onToggleAutofit`) → `RootTopBar` (`app.tsx`) → `TopBar` props (tolerant-empty: absent `onToggleAutofit` ⇒ no toggle). The behavior it controls (equal-share flex layout, hidden resize handles, non-destructive stored-width round-trip) lives in § Board Autofit Toggle.

**Refresh button** (`RefreshButton` in `top-bar.tsx`; `260703-p29w-topbar-refresh-button`): part of the **L3 always-block since `260704-9o7k`** — promoted out of the former terminal-only group into the always-block (a reload is meaningful on every page), rendered between `ThemeToggle` and `HelpLink` and wrapped in the shared `<span className="hidden sm:flex">`, so it shows in **all four modes** at ≥ `sm` (was Terminal-only, immediately after `ClosePaneButton` inside the `currentWindow &&` block, pre-`9o7k`). Its behavior is **byte-for-byte unchanged** by the move. A **plain `<button type="button">`** whose `onClick` does a **full page reload** — plain click `window.location.reload()`; **Shift+click force-reloads** via the exported `forceReload()` helper (a `fetch(location.href, { cache: "reload" })` that overwrites the document's HTTP cache entry, then `reload()` in `.finally` so it fires even offline — Chrome Shift+reload semantics; the legacy `reload(true)` forceGet flag is dead in modern browsers. The fetch races a 3s timeout (`Promise.race`, then `clearTimeout` in `.finally`) so a **stalled** socket that never resolves *or* rejects still reloads — `.catch` alone covers rejection but not an indefinite hang). `aria-label` "Refresh page", `title` "Refresh page (Shift+click: force reload)", carrying the shared cluster className (`min-w-[24px] min-h-[24px] coarse:min-w-[30px] coarse:min-h-[30px] rounded border border-border …`) and a 14×14 `aria-hidden` stroke SVG (lucide `rotate-cw` — a circular arrow + top-right arrowhead, `stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="2"`, round caps/joins) matching the sibling split/close glyphs. It is the in-app recovery affordance for degraded terminal views (stale relay / wedged xterm / SSE drift) where browser chrome is out of reach (PWA/standalone/kiosk). Deliberately **NO spinner / `useOptimisticAction` / `isPending` / `LogoSpinner`, NO `disabled` state, and NO confirmation** (unlike Split / Close) — the page unloads synchronously so a spinner would never meaningfully render, and the reload is non-destructive by design (constitution II/VI: all client state re-derives on load; tmux sessions are unaffected). The same action is also reachable from the command palette as "View: Refresh Page" (see § Boards Command Palette / § Command Palette View actions below). *(Rejected during intake: a `TerminalClient` `key`-bump remount to reconnect just the relay — deferred as a possible follow-up; tmux `respawn-pane` — destructive, kills the running process.)*

**Toolbar button color convention**: All toolbar buttons (top bar and bottom bar) use `text-text-secondary` as their default foreground color. Active toggle states (Ctrl/Alt modifiers when armed, FixedWidthToggle when active) use `text-accent` with accent background. Hover state uses `hover:border-text-secondary` (border highlight). This convention applies to: compose button, theme toggle, fixed-width toggle, split buttons, close pane button, Esc, Tab, Ctrl, Alt, Fn trigger, arrow pad, and ⌘K.

### Window Heading (`WindowHeading` in `top-bar.tsx`, `260703-5ilm`)

The centered, highlighted, editable window heading — the single most important identity on the Terminal route (the tmux window name, e.g. `riff-gallant-jackal`). It gives the window name the prominence of a document title (mental model: browser-tab / editor title bar) and makes rename lowest-friction direct manipulation. Lives in the top bar's center grid cell (§ Chrome (Top Bar) center cell); renders only when `mode === "terminal" && currentWindow`. Since `260704-pr0p-navbar-page-heading-boot-sweep` it is the terminal instance of the universal `PageType: name` heading — a static prefix span sits OUTSIDE the rename button, and the name is driven by the shared boot-sweep primitive (`useBootSweep`/`SweepCells`, § Hover-Animation Vocabulary → boot sweep) that replaced the standalone decode scramble. **The prefix is a static `Window:` in every lens** (§ Heading is a static `Window:`; `260714-uco1` spec-R4 reversal): `WindowHeading` takes a `prefix` prop, but the sole call site now passes the CONSTANT `WINDOW_PREFIX` — the lens-following `terminalHeadingPrefix()` + `WEB_PREFIX`/`CHAT_PREFIX` were retired, and the heading no longer varies by lens (the L1 `ViewSwitcher` shows the lens). The boot-sweep + inline-rename are carried over unchanged. (History: `260714-r7rq` first parametrized the prefix and `260714-t97o-web-view-lens` generalized it to the lens machinery; `260714-uco1` reverted it to a constant. The `prevPrefixRef` + prefix-keyed replay effect that a lens flip once drove is now INERT — a constant prefix can never change — and survives only as a plan-recorded deletion candidate.)

**Two-tone prefix** (`260704-pr0p`): the `Window:` prefix (static in every lens since `260714-uco1`) renders `text-text-secondary` as a **static sibling span outside the rename button/input** (`hidden sm:inline` — mobile keeps just the name) — clicking it never starts an edit, and the button's `aria-label` stays clean. The name keeps `font-semibold text-text-primary`. The prefix's frame states (dim ahead of cursor / typed behind) come from the boot sweep's `prefix` half.

**Three states** (one component):

- **display** — a `<button aria-label="Rename window {name}" title="Click to rename">` rendering the name (via `<SweepCells>` at rest → plain text) at `text-sm font-semibold text-text-primary` (weight-600 + primary color IS the "highlighted" rest state; the surrounding crumbs are secondary, so weight+color alone read as highlighted — no background). `max-w-[16ch] sm:max-w-[28ch] inline-flex items-center coarse:min-h-[30px]` (mobile-leaf touch target), with the name inside an inner `min-w-0 truncate` span — truncation MUST live on the span, not the button: `text-overflow` is inert on a flex container, and flex centering clipped long names on BOTH ends with no ellipsis (`riff-blustery-whale` → `iff-blustery-whal`). Left-anchored, so long names keep their head and cut at the tail; the button itself stays centered in the grid cell. Click enters edit.
- **boot sweep** (was "decode") — the JS sweep from `useBootSweep` (§ Hover-Animation Vocabulary → boot sweep). One inverse-video accent-green cursor at `DECODE_FRAME_MS = 28`ms/cell sweeps `Window:` + space + name; over the prefix it types (TypedLabel states), over the name it churns `DECODE_GLYPHS`. Crucially the heading container NO LONGER flips `text-accent-green` for the whole scramble (`260704-pr0p` rework M2/N2) — green lives ONLY on the per-cell churn/cursor spans inside `SweepCells`; each resolved cell settles to its own REST color (`restCellClass`: prefix → `text-secondary`, name → semibold `text-primary`), so the left-to-right two-tone reveal is visible instead of a uniform green flash. **Guards** (intake A5, all preserved): (a) a `DECODE_HOVER_INTENT_MS = 140`ms hover-intent delay before the sweep starts (cursor transit toward the right buttons doesn't replay it); (b) edit-start stops the sweep and the input binds to the real `name`/`draft` state, never the scrambled DOM text; (c) the sweep replays once whenever the **DISPLAYED name changes** — a `prevNameRef` **seeded `null`** effect keyed on the incoming `name` prop. The null seed is the `260704-pr0p` mount-replay fix (rework M1): the sweep plays ONCE on mount (first name resolution flips `prevNameRef` from `null`), so route navigation between page types animates — AND a committed rename, an SSE external rename, and window navigation all still replay through the same name-change mechanism (this is why the instance is NOT remounted per window — a fresh mount re-seeds `prevNameRef` to `null` and would replay every time / double-play). Skipped entirely under `prefers-reduced-motion` (`prefersReducedMotion()` reads `window.matchMedia`, guarded for jsdom — the rest state IS the reduced-motion state).
- **edit** — an identically-styled inline `<input aria-label="Window name">` (monospace, `text-left font-semibold text-text-primary`, `border-b border-accent`; `text-left` since `260714-uco1` — dropped `text-center` so the name does not jump horizontally on edit entry now that the heading is left-anchored), width sized in `ch` and growing with content (`Math.max(draft.length + 1, 3)ch`), `autoFocus` + select-on-focus. **Enter commits, Escape cancels, blur commits**; empty/whitespace-only trim on commit = cancel (matches the sidebar/dialog trim guard); an unchanged name is also a no-op. Commit calls the shared `useWindowRename()` hook (§ Shared window rename below) — optimistic store rename + toast on error — then optimistically sets the display; the name-change effect replays the sweep when the store-driven `name` prop settles.

**Keyboard path (Constitution V)**: the command-palette `Window: Rename` action dispatches a `window-heading:rename` `CustomEvent` (mirroring `theme-selector:open`); a document-level listener in `WindowHeading` enters inline edit. The former rename **modal dialog was retired** — the palette was its sole entry point; see § Keyboard Shortcuts (the palette rename action) and § Component Conventions (the shared `Dialog`). The `use-dialog-state.ts` window-rename state (`openRenameDialog`/`handleRename`/`executeRenameWindow` + `lastRenameWindowRef` + the `renameWindow` import) was deleted along with the `<Dialog title="Rename window">` JSX in `app.tsx`; only the SESSION rename dialog remains there.

**External-switch cancel**: a `prevIdentityRef` effect keyed on `${server}:${windowId}` cancels an in-progress edit when the window identity changes out from under it (another client / tmux switching the route) — committing the typed name onto the newly-navigated window would rename the wrong window.

### Display-only page headings (`PageHeadingDisplay` in `top-bar.tsx`, `260704-pr0p`)

The board/root/cockpit siblings of `WindowHeading` — a `PageHeadingDisplay({ prefix, name, solo?, ariaLabel })` that renders the same `PageType: name` two-tone identity via the SAME `useBootSweep`/`SweepCells` primitive, but with NO rename affordance (boards/servers have no rename API; cockpit has no instance). The static prefix span is `hidden sm:inline` (same mobile rule as terminal); the `solo` variant (cockpit) renders the single word primary-medium and visible at all breakpoints. Hover replays the sweep behind the 140ms intent; mount + displayed-name-change replay via the same `null`-seeded `prevNameRef` effect; reduced motion skips. **A11y**: the identity carries a STABLE `aria-label` (the churn glyphs are `aria-hidden` inside `SweepCells`) placed on a `role="group"` wrapper — `aria-label` is prohibited on the implicit `role="generic"` of a bare `<div>`/`<span>`, so `role="group"` is what makes it a valid, screen-reader-stable accessible name (`260704-pr0p` rework N3). No `<h1>` is added to the top bar.

**Tests**: `top-bar.test.tsx` covers the heading display/edit states (click → input, Enter commits via `renameWindow`, Escape/empty-trim cancel), the `window-heading:rename` CustomEvent entering edit, AND per-mode heading coverage (terminal `Window:` prefix sibling — `Window:` since `260714-uco1`, board `Board:` + board switcher in the center, root `Server Cabin:`, solo `Cockpit`; board left nav shows only counts/hint — no `Board ▸`, no left board name; root left nav has no `aria-current` leaf). E2e `tests/e2e/window-heading.spec.ts` (+ sibling `.spec.md`, per the constitution's Test Companion Docs rule) covers, documented 1:1 in the `.spec.md`: the terminal heading renders the name once with a static `Window:` prefix sibling (NOT a trailing breadcrumb crumb); click → inline input → Enter commits (sidebar + heading reflect the new name); Escape cancels (window id unchanged); the palette `window-heading:rename` CustomEvent enters inline edit; the 375px bar stays single-line with no horizontal overflow; hover-treatment classes present and unchanged under `reducedMotion: "reduce"`; the board/root/cockpit centered headings render with their prefixes; the `[ SESSIONS▊ ]` section-heading shape; a motion-opted-in **boot-sweep** e2e (hover the heading → an `.rk-typed-cursor` cell attaches → resolves to rest — `260704-pr0p` SHOULD-FIX 2, since the units stub `matchMedia` to reduced-motion and never exercise the sweep behaviorally); and a reduced-context check that the sweep never starts (JS-gated).

### Shared window rename (`useWindowRename`, `hooks/use-window-rename.ts`, `260703-5ilm`)

`useWindowRename()` returns `execute(server, session, windowId, newName)` — the ONE optimistic window-rename action, used by BOTH the top-bar `WindowHeading` AND the sidebar inline rename (`sidebar/index.tsx:398`), so the two surfaces rename identically. It stamps the window store's `pendingName` (`renameWindow`) on `onOptimistic`, rolls back via `clearRename` on failure with a toast, and clears the pending marker on settle (SSE snapshot then becomes authoritative). The captured `(server, session, windowId)` is held in a `lastRenameRef` so rollback/settle target the right entry even if the caller re-renders between execute and resolution. Callers own their own trim/empty-name guards before calling (rename is unconditional inside the hook). This extraction replaced the sidebar's former inline ~25-line `executeRenameWindow` `useOptimisticAction` block (deleted by `260703-5ilm`). Session rename is NOT part of this hook — it keeps its own dialog/inline path (§ Sidebar → Session rename).

### Hover-Animation Vocabulary (`260703-5ilm`)

A site-wide motion map where each treatment encodes **exactly one** category of element, so motion carries meaning instead of noise. The shared color cue: **the animated element turns `--color-accent-green` while it animates** (the brand chip on glitch-hover, the boot-sweep cursor + name-churn cells, both caret variants, the stepping brackets — user-requested — including the glint: the sweep strip is accent-green-tinted and the hovered chip's border + glyph flip green for the hover duration, the "green line"). **Scope note** (`260704-pr0p`): the boot-sweep green is now PER-CELL — only the single cursor cell and the unresolved name-churn glyphs are green; the heading container does NOT tint green wholesale (the earlier decode did), so resolved cells settle to their own rest color and the two-tone reveal reads left-to-right. All utilities live in `globals.css` (beside the `logo-chase` keyframes / `coarse` variant; Tailwind CSS 4). Under `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)` the contract is **animations zeroed, not styling removed**: the CSS gate zeroes every keyframe animation (classes stay in the DOM — that is the test seam), the JS treatments (decode, typed sweep) skip themselves by reading the same media query, and static hover styling (e.g. the glint's green border/glyph flip) remains — a color change is not motion. No pixel assertions in tests — treatments are asserted via class-presence + reduced-motion emulation, plus one behavioral guard for the caret (below).

| Category | Treatment | Mechanism |
|----------|-----------|-----------|
| **Brand** | glitch | `.rk-brand-glitch` on the top-left "Run Kit" brand anchor — one-shot `@keyframes rk-glitch` RGB-split `text-shadow` (~300ms, `steps(2)`, ±2px split) on `:hover`, plus `color: var(--color-accent-green)` for the hover duration (the color snap is what makes the glitch read at 11.5px; the split is texture — the shadow alone was barely visible). Wordmark hidden below `sm`, so on mobile only the icon jitters (accepted). |
| **Top-bar page heading** | boot sweep | JS in `top-bar.tsx` — the shared `useBootSweep` hook + `SweepCells` renderer (see § Window Heading / § Display-only page headings), NOT a CSS class. ONE inverse-video accent-green cursor at `DECODE_FRAME_MS` (28ms/cell) sweeps `PageType:` + space + `name`: over the PREFIX it types like TypedLabel (`rk-typed-off` ahead / `rk-typed-cursor` cursor cell / `text-secondary` resolved); over the NAME the cells right of the cursor churn `DECODE_GLYPHS` in accent-green from frame 0, each locked to its true char as the cursor arrives, resolved cells settling to semibold `text-primary` (spaces preserved). Reuses the `rk-typed-*` cell classes + `DECODE_*` constants — no class of its own. Replaced `260703-5ilm`'s terminal-only "decode" scramble (which flipped the whole heading green). |
| **Section headings** | brackets + caret | `.rk-bracket-group` scoped to `SectionHeading`'s inner bracket cluster ONLY (not the row/rule/`side`). On group `:hover` the `.rk-bracket-open`/`.rk-bracket-close` spans step outward `translateX(∓3px)` + turn `--color-accent-green` (transform only — no layout shift), and a `.rk-bracket-caret` (always-reserved `1ch` cell, accent-green, transparent at rest so the closing bracket never shifts) blinks `▊` (`@keyframes rk-caret-blink`, 1.06s `steps(1)`). Moved from the retired `PageHeading` to the in-page section labels by `260704-pr0p`. See § Section Heading. |
| **Section labels** | typed sweep | `TypedLabel` (`components/typed-label.tsx`) — on hover the label fades (`.rk-typed-off`, 26% opacity) and an inverse-video cursor (`.rk-typed-cursor`, accent-green cell OVER the character — a terminal block cursor sitting on text) sweeps from the FIRST cell, "typing" each character back to full brightness (`.rk-typed-on`); after the pass the label holds bright (`rk-typed-done`) until pointer-leave. Fixed ~350ms TOTAL pass regardless of length (per-cell = 350/len clamped 20–60ms) so all labels read as one gesture; width never changes (the cursor occupies its cell). JS-driven (the frame states are the `globals.css` `.rk-typed-*` classes); reduced motion skips the sweep entirely in JS. Applied to the sidebar panel titles (`collapsible-panel.tsx`) and the sidebar `Sessions` region heading (`sidebar/index.tsx`) directly, and — since `260704-pr0p` wrapped them in `SectionHeading` — INSIDE the brackets on the Server Cabin `Sessions` heading (`session-tiles.tsx`) and the four Cockpit zone `h2`s (Host Health / Boards / Tmux Servers / Services, `server-list-page.tsx`), where the typed sweep and the brackets+caret hover compose on one element. The sidebar labels are deliberately NOT bracket targets (typed-sweep only). Decorative — headings stay non-interactive-looking at rest. |
| **Buttons** | CRT glint + green line | `.rk-glint` — `position:relative; overflow:hidden` + an `::after` skewed accent-green highlight strip sweeping across the button face on `:hover` (`@keyframes rk-glint-sweep`, ~450ms one-shot), plus `.rk-glint:hover:not(:disabled)` flipping border + glyph to `--color-accent-green` (unlayered rule, so it beats the chips' Tailwind hover utilities without touching call sites; chosen over a fill/inverse cell so hover never reads as the armed state's solid accent fill). Applied to every top-bar right-cluster chip (SplitButton, ClosePaneButton, TerminalFontControl, NotificationControl, ThemeToggle, FixedWidthToggle, BoardAutofitToggle, HelpLink) AND the bottom-bar `KBD_CLASS` buttons. `overflow:hidden` is verified safe — the font/bell popovers are SIBLINGS of their trigger buttons, not children, so clipping never clips a popover. |

**Typed-sweep history note**: the section-label treatment was originally a CSS-only hover caret (`.rk-label-caret::after`), replaced wholesale by the `TypedLabel` typed sweep after a design iteration (user picked the inverse-video-cursor variation from the heading-lab demo). The old CSS classes are deleted; the e2e guard now asserts the sweep behaviorally (cursor cell attaches → `rk-typed-done` lands → unhover resets). The `.rk-bracket-caret` is unrelated and unchanged — a reserved `1ch` blinking caret cell inside the bracket group, now carried by `SectionHeading` (was `PageHeading`, `260704-pr0p`). Note the section labels now compose BOTH vocabularies on one element: the typed sweep (TypedLabel, inside the brackets) AND the brackets+caret hover (the `rk-bracket-group` cluster around them).

### Theme System

> Full spec: [`docs/specs/themes.md`](../../specs/themes.md) — architecture, ANSI palette structure, tmux colour mapping, import script usage, persistence model.

Palette-based theme model: each theme defines a `ThemePalette` with 22 canonical terminal colors — `foreground`, `background`, `cursorColor`, `cursorText`, `selectionBackground`, `selectionForeground`, plus 16 ANSI colors (indices 0-15) as a fixed-length readonly tuple. The `Theme` type has shape `{ id, name, category, palette }` — no `colors` or `themeColor` properties (both replaced by derivation from palette).

20 built-in themes (14 dark + 6 light) defined in `app/frontend/src/themes.ts` with canonical ANSI palettes sourced from iTerm2-Color-Schemes / official theme repos. Three consumers derive from the same palette:

1. **Web UI CSS** — `deriveUIColors(palette, category)` produces 8 `UIColors` keys (`bgPrimary`, `bgCard`, `bgInset`, `textPrimary`, `textSecondary`, `border`, `accent`, `accentGreen`). Derivation: `bgPrimary` = background, `bgCard` = lighten/darken background, `bgInset` = darken background, `textPrimary` = foreground, `textSecondary` = ansi[8] (bright black), `border` = blend(fg, bg, 0.25), `accent` = ansi[4] (blue), `accentGreen` = ansi[2] (green). Color utility helpers (`hexToRgb`, `rgbToHex`, `lightenHex`, `darkenHex`, `blendHex`) are module-private. CSS custom properties (`--color-bg-primary`, etc.) applied via inline styles on `document.documentElement.style` overriding `globals.css` fallbacks.
2. **xterm.js canvas** — `deriveXtermTheme(palette)` produces an xterm.js `ITheme` with all 22 colors mapped (background, foreground, cursor, cursorAccent, selectionBackground, selectionForeground, and 16 named ANSI colors black through brightWhite). Terminal content (syntax highlighting, colored prompts, git diff output) matches the selected theme.
3. **tmux chrome** — `configs/tmux/default.conf` uses ANSI `colour{N}` indices (colour0-colour15) instead of hardcoded hex. Because tmux renders its chrome as escape sequences that xterm.js interprets, changing the xterm.js ANSI palette automatically themes tmux status bar, pane borders, and pane-border-format. No runtime `tmux set -g` calls needed — the tmux.conf is static.

`data-theme` attribute set to theme's `category` ("dark" or "light") for CSS branching. Theme preferences persisted to both backend API (`GET/PUT /api/settings/theme` writing `~/.rk/settings.yaml`) and localStorage as synchronous cache. Three settings: `theme` (mode: `"system"` or specific ID), `theme_dark` (preferred dark theme, default `"default-dark"`), `theme_light` (preferred light theme, default `"default-light"`). localStorage keys: `runkit-theme`, `runkit-theme-dark`, `runkit-theme-light`. On init, API is canonical source; localStorage is the fast fallback if API fails. Unrecognized `theme` values fall back to `"system"`, while unrecognized `theme_dark`/`theme_light` values fall back to `"default-dark"`/`"default-light"`. PUT accepts partial updates (load-then-merge).

**ThemeToggle** (top bar): Normal click cycles `system → default-light → default-dark`. **Ctrl+Click / Cmd+Click** dispatches `"theme-selector:open"` CustomEvent to open the theme selector.

**Theme Selector** (`app/frontend/src/components/theme-selector.tsx`): Modal overlay matching CommandPalette structure (fixed z-50, backdrop, max-w-lg at 20vh). Search input filters by name (case-insensitive). Themes grouped under "Dark" / "Light" category headers. Arrow key navigation wraps and skips headers. Mouse hover and arrow navigation trigger live preview via `previewTheme()` — CSS custom properties update in real-time. Enter confirms (persists to API + localStorage), Escape/outside-click reverts to original theme via `cancelPreview()`. Opens via `"theme-selector:open"` custom event (same pattern as `"palette:open"`). Theme rows display multi-color palette swatches showing background plus representative ANSI colors (red, green, yellow, blue, magenta, cyan) instead of a single-color swatch.

**Command palette**: "Theme: Select Theme" action dispatches `"theme-selector:open"`. Individual "Theme: System", "Theme: Light", "Theme: Dark" quick-switch actions retained.

**ThemeProvider** (`app/frontend/src/contexts/theme-context.tsx`): `useTheme()` returns `{ preference, resolved, theme, themeDark, themeLight }`. `useThemeActions()` returns `{ setTheme, previewTheme, cancelPreview }`. Preview applies colors to DOM without persistence. Cancel reverts to the last persisted theme. Uses stable `actionsRef` pattern for callback identity. On init: calls `getThemePreference()` from API (returns `{ theme, themeDark, themeLight }`), falls back to localStorage / defaults if API fails. Per-mode theme resolution: in `"system"` mode, resolves to the user's preferred dark or light theme based on OS `prefers-color-scheme`, falling back to `DEFAULT_DARK_THEME` / `DEFAULT_LIGHT_THEME` if the stored ID is invalid. `setTheme` with a specific theme ID saves it to the matching per-mode slot (by `category`), keeps preference as `"system"` (preserving OS auto-toggle), and persists all three values to API and localStorage. `setTheme("system")` resets to system mode without changing per-mode prefs. Backend is canonical source of truth; localStorage is the fast fallback.

### Breadcrumb Dropdowns

Session and window name text are the dropdown triggers. Clicking/tapping the name opens the respective dropdown. No split click-target pattern — the name itself is the trigger. The session name shown in the breadcrumb is the **snapshot-derived** owning session of the active `@N` (since `260529-jad6` dropped `$session` from the URL), not a URL segment.

**Session dropdown**: Lists all tmux sessions. Current session highlighted with `text-accent`. Selecting navigates to the session's first window by its window ID (`/{server}/{windows[0].windowId}` — 2-segment since `260529-jad6`). First item: `+ New Session` action — triggers instant session creation (no dialog).

**Window switcher** (relocated out of the breadcrumb by `260703-5ilm`): Lists all windows in the current session. Current window highlighted (`w.windowId === currentWindow.windowId`). Selecting navigates to `/{server}/{windowId}` (2-segment since `260529-jad6`). First item: `+ New Window` action (creates new window in current session). **No longer a trailing breadcrumb crumb** — it now renders as a **label-less bare-`▾` `BreadcrumbDropdown`** in the top bar's center cell, beside the centered `WindowHeading` (name-click = edit, `▾`-click = switch); the window name lives once in the heading. Still carries `title="Window"` and stays visible on mobile (the only in-bar window switcher once the crumb moved). See § Chrome (Top Bar) center cell / § Window Heading.

**Board switcher** (`BoardSwitcher` in `top-bar.tsx`, relocated to the center cell by `260704-pr0p-navbar-page-heading-boot-sweep`): the board mode's `▾` dropdown — lists the cross-server boards + a `← Sessions` navigate action. Moved from the left `BoardModeBreadcrumb` (the old `Board ▸ {name} ▾` cluster) to sit beside the centered `Board: <board>` display heading, mirroring the window switcher's center-cell placement. The board name is display-only (no rename API); the `▾` is the sole board affordance in the bar. The left nav keeps only the pane/server counts + `⌘[⌘] cycle` hint (`BoardModeInfo`). See § Chrome (Top Bar) center cell / Board.

**Action items in dropdowns**: `BreadcrumbDropdown` accepts an optional `action` prop of type `{ label: string; onAction: () => void }`. When provided, the action item renders before the selection list, separated by a divider (`border-t border-border`). Action items use `text-text-primary` styling (not `text-accent`), close the dropdown on click, and are excluded from ArrowUp/ArrowDown keyboard navigation among selection items.

**Optional `secondaryAction`** (since `260713-sbk1-web-spawn-agent`): a second leading action of the same `{ label, onAction }` shape, rendered below `action` and above the divider — **only honored when `action` is also present**. Its sole call site is the terminal-mode window-switcher dropdown, which renders `+ New Window` (`action`) and `+ New Agent` (`secondaryAction`) as two stacked leading buttons. The two actions occupy dropdown indices `0..offset-1` (leading actions) with selection items following at `offset..N-1`; the internal `actionRef` singleton became an `actionRefs` array and the focus-index `offset` is now the count of present leading actions — so the keyboard-nav index math generalizes to N leading actions while every **other** call site (session switcher, board switcher) that passes only `action` keeps its single-action behavior byte-for-byte. This minimal second-prop shape was chosen over a generic `actions: []` array (only one call site needs two actions, and an array would churn every call site plus the focus-index logic). See § Spawn-Agent Dialog.

**Dropdown component** (`app/frontend/src/components/breadcrumb-dropdown.tsx`): Reusable dropdown with outside-click dismiss, Escape dismiss, ArrowUp/ArrowDown keyboard navigation, ARIA `role="menu"`/`role="menuitem"`. Styled with `bg-bg-primary border-border shadow-2xl`, matching bottom-bar Fn key dropdown pattern. Name text serves as the trigger (44px on touch devices via `coarse:min-h-[44px]`), wrapped in a `min-w-0 truncate` span. When the trigger has a label (`icon` prop set) it renders a **persistent `▾` caret** after the label (`aria-hidden`, `ml-1 shrink-0 text-base` — 16px, user-tuned for visibility) — the always-visible "opens a menu" affordance distinguishing dropdown crumbs from link crumbs (`260702-6m46`; see § Crumb Affordance Vocabulary). A label-less trigger already IS a bare caret (`▾` fallback) and gets no second one. Long names truncated via `max-w-[240px]`.

Connection indicator: green/gray dot only (no text label), driven by `isConnected` from ChromeProvider (set by each page from `useSessions`).

### Crumb Affordance Vocabulary (`260702-6m46`)

Breadcrumb crumbs advertise their interactivity WITHOUT hover — a two-affordance vocabulary where the crumbs that remain are all interactive (since `260704-pr0p-navbar-page-heading-boot-sweep` moved every current-page LEAF out of the left nav into the centered heading, § Chrome (Top Bar), the "you are here" signal is the centered heading itself, not a no-affordance crumb). The cases:

- **Link crumbs** (brand, server link) — carry the shared `LINK_CRUMB_CLASS` constant (`top-bar.tsx`): a **bordered chip** (`rounded border border-border hover:border-text-secondary px-1.5 py-0.5 text-text-secondary hover:text-text-primary transition-colors`), reusing the right cluster's "bordered = clickable" language. The user compared three candidates live (chip / accent color / dotted underline) and picked the chip; the unused variant definitions were removed at lock-in. *(Accent color was rejected — hue is reserved by the StatusDot phases; dotted underline was rejected — it left the mobile icon-only brand with no affordance, and text-decoration doesn't propagate into an anchor's flex children, so the wordmark needed a `[text-decoration:inherit]` patch that the chip doesn't.)*
- **Dropdown triggers** (session — and the relocated window/board switchers) — carry the persistent `▾` caret inside `BreadcrumbDropdown` (see § Breadcrumb Dropdowns). Signals "opens a switcher", distinct from "navigates". Note the **window switcher** (since `260703-5ilm`) AND the **board switcher** (since `260704-pr0p`) are no longer in the left breadcrumb — both are bare-`▾` `BreadcrumbDropdown`s in the top bar's center cell beside their headings (§ Chrome (Top Bar) center cell), using the same caret affordance.
- **Current-page leaf** — since `260704-pr0p` there is NO leaf crumb in the left nav; the current page's identity is the **centered `PageType: name` heading**. The former `aria-current="page"` server-name leaf on Server Cabin moved to the center as `Server Cabin: <server>`. (The historical "the absence of an affordance marks the leaf" case no longer applies to a crumb — the heading carries the "you are here" role.)

*Why not hover-only cues*: the pre-`260702-6m46` `hover:text-text-primary` cue was invisible to first-time users and absent entirely on touch.

### Section Heading (`section-heading.tsx`, `260704-pr0p`; retired `page-heading.tsx`)

A shared `SectionHeading({ label, side?, className? })` renders a one-line **bracketed BBS-menu-tag** SECTION heading — `[ SESSIONS▊ ]──────────── side`. It is the successor to the retired `PageHeading` (`page-heading.tsx` + `page-heading.test.tsx` DELETED by `260704-pr0p-navbar-page-heading-boot-sweep`): the bracket idiom that used to name the PAGE in the page body now names in-page SECTIONS, because page identity moved to the top-bar center heading (§ Chrome (Top Bar), § Canonical page names — Vocabulary Split).
